Origin and Etymology of <i>man</i>    </h2>      <div class="card-primary-content">      <p>        <div class="et"><!--  --><!--    --><!--      -->Middle English, from Old English <em class="mw_t_it">man, mon</em> human being, male human; akin to Old High German <em class="mw_t_it">man</em> human being, Sanskrit <em class="mw_t_it">manu</em><!--    --><!--  --><!----></div>
